< review>
This is just off of the trail. There are large grassy areas, playground equipment, shade trees, and shelters. The shelters are reserved in advance and the weekends can be busy. Just stop by to kick a soccer ball or play in the equipment. The bathrooms are public and can be clean or bad - depends in the users and their willingness to be respectful.  The trail connected is a good path for walks, runs, or rides. Bicyclists should yield to those walking.< /review>

<text>This place has a strange dive bar quality to it that I like. It's not fancy and it's not in a great area but the food is good. The first time there I had 2 Carne Asada soft tacos to go. They were very good. Inside they have a covered salsa bar with some fiery salsas. Go easy until you are comfortable with the spice level of the salsas. I used only a little. I tried the red salsa and the brown one. Both were hot. The next time there I got the Carne Asada plate (number 8). The tacos were the same as before but it included rice and beans for a few dollars more. Maybe a better deal to just get the tacos alone and save the extra $3 or $4? The inside of the restaurant is pleasant (in a dive bar kind of way) and the service was good. I'll be back.</text>< Rate>

< review>
We love the vibe at the Inn at Moonlight Beach. Not only is the staff extremely attentive, the location of the Inn is terrific. We walked and biked each day we were there. We added a snack, champagne and massage package that was totally worth it. The  breakfast each morning was delicious and we purchased many of the homemade honey and teas to bring home as gifts. The grounds are meticulously landscaped and provide a zen space for you to relax.</review>

<user_name>Mary Mikolich< /user_name><Time>1614118174379< /Time><Rate>5</Rate><review>Calming carefully appointed room with a soothing vibe, ocean view from the patio, attentive staff and great location.</review><Pics>None</Pics>< Resp>

< review>
Tucked away in a lush garden setting on the side of a hill lies this wonderful retreat that focuses on connecting with nature and with oneself. We had a one night reservation so we got there right around the 3pm check-in time to make the most of our stay.  The staff was very welcoming and friendly. The property was smaller than I thought it would be, but the fact that the Inn is only a 6 room bed and breakfast adds to the intimacy of the place, and made it feel so cozy. The property and our room was so clean, and the Covid measures they had in place felt very safe and made me feel comfortable. We stayed in the Rosemary room which is one of the rooms on the bottom level. The room had an outside deck to sit at which overlooked the outside gardens which is a shared common space for the other rooms as well. A couple of guests were enjoying the outside table next to the water feature the next morning, but that did not bother me, and the deck still felt fairly private at night. The garden was lovely to walk through and you can feel free to clip some fresh herbs from the garden to enjoy at home. There are many succulent plants growing there, and you can purchase them to take home, with the smallest plants starting at two dollars.
The holistic vibe continues with a focus on the healing energy of nature such as through crystals, for instance there is a large selenite globe in your room, and you can purchase other crystals from the small display cases in the lobby. I purchased some honey, fresh preserves, and bath salts to take home. The room was very comfortable with a sitting area, and a nice kitchenette including a microwave, dishes, and utensils.
The bed was very comfy and I slept wonderfully. The humidifier, and the sound machine, which you could change to hear sounds of the ocean, rainfall, etc, added to the relaxing vibe. There was a very large flat screen TV, but did not feel the need to turn it on because it was so peaceful just listening to the sound machine, or my bluetooth speaker I brought from home, or the croaking of the frogs out in the garden at night. The included herbal flower tea bath set was a great way to end the day in the deep soak bathtub, tea light candles are also provided to add to the ambiance. The included fresh herbal tea setup served in a clear glass kettle that is kept warm over a tea light burner, as well as a snack plate with dried fruits, nuts, and organic chocolates, is a lovely welcome in your room upon check in. Breakfast is delivered outside your room in the morning. It is not a hot breakfast, but was still a very delicious assortment of items such as yogurt parfaits, bakery goods, fruit, and boiled eggs, which you can pre-select the night before. In addition to the many complimentary offers, the availability of the various add-ons is a great way to enhance the experience of your stay. For my birthday stay here I added the herbal foot soak which is enjoyed out on the deck, and was served with more hot herbal tea to enjoy. I also added the Full Moon package which included extras such as a large charcuterie board, sparkling wine, a large fresh flower bouquet from the garden, a meditation kit including items such as a selenite stone, and complementary late checkout.  The Inn is a short walk to Moonlight Beach, be sure to stop at the very unique rock garden on your way there. The nearby Cottonwood Creek park was lovely to stroll through, and downtown Encinitas is a short walk away as well. Just be advised that there is no sidewalk from the Inn down to the street corner, so be aware of cars, or when walking at night. I walked to nearby Chiko, they served delicious Asian fusion cuisine and brought it back to our room, but you can also have food delivered to the Inn from one of the nearby restaurants if you don‚Äôt want to walk at night. I would highly recommend the Inn at Moonlight Beach for anyone looking for a peaceful place to relax and recharge!< /review>

My boyfriend and I stayed at the Inn at Moonlight Beach for his 50th birthday.  We felt that based on the size of the property and the commitment to wellness that we would be safe here.  It was tranquil and blissful.  The rooms are spacious, clean and well air-conditioned. The patio off of our room was beautiful, comfortable and peaceful. I loved our bathtub. I arranged for a charcuterie board for our arrival. It was abundant with cheese, meats, fruits and nuts. The Inn provided bags of herbs and real flowers to put in the bath. That was a fabulous experience. The kitchenette is well stocked with amenities. The breakfast was delicious. The owner was on hand to give us a tour of the property. We picked fruit grown on the property in their bio-dynamic farm. There is also a firepit and seating area to enjoy an evening outdoors with smores. Yum. We loved that.  The main drag of town, Encinitas, is just a few blocks away as is the beach.  We had dinner in Encinitas during our stay and went to the beach prior to the arrival. It was a wonderful experience.  We cannot wait to go back.</Review>

Very nice rooms and common areas inside. It is closer to a busy road than we realized, so it's a bit noisy with the patio door open. PURE MAGIC. If you are looking for a sacred, grounding, rejuvenating, relaxing, beautifully energetic space filled with love, grace and peace‚Ä¶.this is your spot. This hidden gem will truly amaze you and let me share why‚Ä¶

I was intrigued to learn from our lovely hostess (who actually is the amazing architect of this sacred space) that this Inn actually meets WELL building standards which means that the space itself enhances human heath and well-being through design and operational features of the environment (such as the biodynamic gardens, water, air, atmosphere and lighting). WELL building standards look into the connection between the physical building and the wellbeing of whomever inherits the space. SO COOL and inspirational that buildings can actually leave people and the environment better off than before they spent time in the building.

THE COMMON SPACE: One of my favorite parts of the space is the communal living room and kitchen hang out area. This space is soooo lovely, inviting and calming. It has an amazing indoor-outdoor feel to it with the ambiance sounds and decor that made me feel very connected to nature. There are all sorts of healing herbal teas, spices, roots and herbs, snacks, fruit and vegetables from the on-site gardens and the most amazing coffee! It is a help-yourself style kitchen and so you feel like you are home, which is such a unique experience for an Inn environment. There is also an extensive book shelf with a range of books that bring insight, awareness and inspiration to your life! The yoga deck is another feature that I truly appreciated having available.

THE ROOM: #FengShuiAllDay! WOW - another amazing, oh so cozy and comforting, beautiful space. I stayed in the Sage room - Ocean view balcony ‚Ä¶ need I say any more? I bring my own pillow with me everywhere and I actually forgot my pillow and I was so pleased that these pillows beat my own pillow times 10! So luxurious. I had everything I needed! In the morning a picnic basket filled with all sorts of delicious complimentary breakfast goodies was waiting on my doorstep! This was a perfect place for a romantic stay with my boyfriend :) I‚Äôd also consider coming here for a weekend meditation retreat or for a rejuvenation weekend.

I had such an experience of being welcomed and at home in the grace of contribution and love from our exceptional hostess, the lovely inn keeper and from the environment itself. Inn at Moonlight deserves a 10 star rating from me!!! :)

I hope anyone reading this enjoys his or her stay as much as I did! You will be left feeling peaceful, connected and powerful after your stay. Enjoy! :)<//Text>

This is the largest and cleanest laundromat I've ever visited. There are machines ranging from $2.50 or $2.75 top loaders to $9 for an 8 load front loader. And there are plenty of dryers of standard and xl sizes. Folding tables, seating, restrooms, change machines, and there's always someone there working or staffing their "store" where you can buy all laundry needs and even snacks & drinks. Nice, clean, new laundry spot. Attendant Diane is the most meticulous cleaner of all the employees I've met. Number of free dryers need to be increased especially during this pandemic. The small area of free dry is so clustered together it's almost not worth it considering the virus. You can buy individual detergent pods, small detergent bottles, softeners, dryer sheets etc at the office window. You can conveniently use your iPhone or Android to download their app and directly load your laundry money to the app from your debit card. <Review>My girlfriend's Macbook Air started randomly shutting down for no foreseeable reason, so we did a google search for macbook repair places, and BDJ came up. She brought the laptop in and met with Jose (without me - I had to work). He was a little rough around the edges from the get go, but seemed to know what he was doing. He opened her laptop and told her to feel the processor, trying to support his diagnosis of overheating being the problem. This was the first sign of trouble, as anyone who works on computers knows that feeling a processor will not tell you if it's overheating as processors often get above 150 degrees while staying within normal range of operation. He told her that the fix was to replace the logic board and that it this would cost ~$350.  She paid, and he told her he had to order the logic board and that she should bring the laptop back after he called us to let us know it had arrived.

She came home and we looked at her laptop. I did some of the diagnostic stuff they do at the Apple store and it quickly became apparent that this was a battery/charger issue and most likely had nothing to do with the logic board. I called and spoke to Jose to try explain my thoughts and perhaps get a refund for the $350 she had already paid since a battery replacement wouldn't be this much. He immediately started becoming VERY agitated and trying to rush me off the phone, saying he had other customers he had to help. He kept insisting that the logic board was the issue. The longer I kept him on the phone trying to explain the logic behind my theory, the more and more rude he became, explaining that "I told your girl to feel the processor. I told her! Have her explain to you! I don't have time. I have other customers here to take care of!" I asked him if he would refund the money if he did indeed replace the logic board, and it turned out that wasn't the issue, and he promised he would provide the refund.

Flash forward 2-weeks, I called again to see if the logic board had come in. It took him 3 tries to find the correct customer account after I gave him the invoice number he provided when we paid. He explained that the logic board had arrived and that we could bring the laptop in. We dropped it off the next day, and he called 3 days later to say the work was done.

Upon bringing the Macbook home, within the first hour or so, it began randomly shutting down just like before. I ordered a new genuine Apple magsafe charger, and low-and-behold, it stopped shutting down and everything was fine once again. This of course proved my theory that it was a power issue and not the logic board. I called Jose back and tried to explain this. He almost immediately became irate and started making all sorts of strange claims. One, he said that he was not able to test the laptop because my girlfriend "never gave him her password". He never once asked for said password, as we would have obliged if it meant he would be able to fix the issue. He then told me to bring the laptop back in, but by then, I was so appalled by the way he had spoken to me that I told him I did not want to do business with him anymore and asked that he please provide the refund he originally promised. He declined and repeated that I needed to bring the computer back in. I spent about 10 minutes on the phone with him, trying to reason with him, politely asking for the refund, explaining how what he had done did not fix the issue and how a simple charger replacement did the trick. He would not hear it and began using the "I have other customers I have to take care of" line as before. Finally, he one last time said "You want help, bring the computer back in!" and hung up the phone.

We didn't bring it back to him. As a paying customer, I've never been spoken to like Jose spoke to me on the phone, and I would highly recommend you stay away from this place. There are plenty of other Apple repair shops in the valley. You may pay a bit more elsewhere, but at least you'll avoid getting yelled at and lied to.<//Review>< name>

< Text>
I had a great experience with BDJ Repair. I spilled water on my MacBook Pro keyboard and the laptop stopped powering on. I know my way around computers ‚Äî I can take my MacBook apart and replace the keyboard, for example‚Äîbut a logic board repair is beyond what I can do. I researched online and based on reviews, price, and the info on the BDJ website I chose to come here, even though I am in southern Orange County and the shop is an hour away. I was impressed that BDJ does all of their own work in house, including very technical BGA reballing soldering. That indicated a certain level of expertise.

When I walked in on Monday they initially said it would be ready on Thursday. They are a busy shop and I could see how many machines they had to work on. I was leaving the country and asked for an expedited delivery time. They said no promises, but would have it down on Wednesday afternoon, "maybe" Tuesday night. However, on Tuesday morning I already had a response that the laptop was ready. W O W.

<rate>5< /rate><review>When I was growing up, in the 1960s, if the family television began to act up my father would remove the tubes, take them down to the drugstore, diagnose the bad tube and replace it.  Component level repair was the norm.  Sometime during the 70's or 80's  we as a nation seemed to collectively forget  how to repair our products at the component level and, with computers in particular, when a component fails (e.g. a surface mounted IC), we toss out the entire board and replace it --- throwing away hundreds of working components.  This is wasteful, costly, lazy and stupid.

Jose at BDJ is a talented technician who diagnoses which component on a board has failed and uses special manufacturing tools (surface mount IC) to replace just the component.  A repair to my system board that would have cost $750 anywhere else, cost just $200 here.  It was completed in two work days with a smile and not a promise broken.

Go to BDJ, not just to save a few hundred bucks (you will), but to help save the environment from excessive waste and help save the country from stupidity.  Thanks Jose!</review>< Pictures>
